========================================================================
RED-TEAM REVIEW — dCDF v5 (PRTOE_v5_dCDF_complete.md)
Reviewer: Claude (Opus 4.8), adversarial pass
Turn 1 of a dialogue. Defender: please answer inline under each item.
========================================================================

Framing for the defender: I have read the complete v5 document. I am not
here to relitigate the arithmetic — the null test, the β execution, the
gauge-IC fix, the tolerance discovery are all clean and I concede them.
I am here to attack the *thesis*, not the bookkeeping. Each item below
forces a choice: produce the concrete object I ask for, or concede the
point in writing. "It's an open item (§11)" is not an answer to any of
these — I am asking whether the open items are *closable*, or whether
they are load-bearing walls disguised as to-dos.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ATTACK 1 — THE UNFALSIFIABILITY PINCER (the one I most want answered)
------------------------------------------------------------------------
§4.2 proves the fluid is EXACTLY ΛCDM-degenerate at background and linear
order. §10a concedes the nonlinear regime is out of scope — c_s²=0 gives
single-valued ∇φ, caustics at first shell-crossing, "virialized structure
unproven." So the model is identical to ΛCDM everywhere it can be computed,
and uncomputable everywhere it might differ.

Name ONE observable — existing or future, linear or nonlinear, cosmological
or astrophysical — that could, even in principle, return the answer "dCDF"
rather than "ΛCDM" or "ΛCDM + standard extensions." A single discriminating
measurement. If you cannot name one, then concede in writing that dCDF is at
present not a falsifiable physical model but a reparametrization of ΛCDM with
a narrative attached — elegant, but metaphysics until the discriminator
exists. (Note: "the a^-6 stiff tail / BBN basin-entry signature" from §2 is
a signature of the *completion*, not of the fluid EoS you actually fit — if
that is your answer, say so explicitly and accept that it makes the
completion, not dCDF, the falsifiable object.)

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ATTACK 2 — THE FLUID CONTRIBUTES ZERO TO THE FIT
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Every χ² gain you report is carried by ξ_Neff and (now) m_e — both, in your
own words, "ordinary phenomenology any same-parameter extension would
produce." The dCDF *fluid* contributes exactly nothing to any likelihood.

Question: what does "ΛCDM, with ω_cdm and Λ replaced by one dark fluid" buy
over "ΛCDM + N_eff + varying m_e" — same parameter count, same fits, no
fluid? You claim "parameter economy." Demonstrate it as a number: write the
Bayesian evidence difference attributable to the unification ALONE, with
ξ and m_e held identical in both models. If that number is ≈ 0 (and §4.2
implies it must be), then the economy is aesthetic, not statistical, and
you should stop listing it as a benefit.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ATTACK 3 — THE HONEST EVIDENCE IS ALREADY NEGATIVE
------------------------------------------------------------------------
On the decisive (joint) stack: Δχ² ≈ 0 tie, minus ξ's Occam penalty (~2),
plus the m_e credit — but the CONTROLLED m_e credit is −1 to −3, not the
slack-inflated −8.5 — plus a BBN charge of +3.5 that no likelihood in the
stack prices. Sum the honest ledger and dCDF is behind ΛCDM on the only
data that matters.

Steelman the opposite. Give me the single strongest quantitative reason a
referee should read the joint-stack evidence as anything other than "mild
flexible-model tax, ΛCDM preferred." If your best answer is "wait for
PolyChord," concede that the χ²-level ledger is currently ΛCDM-favored and
you are hoping marginalization rescues you.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ATTACK 4 — THE COMPLETION IS NOT A THEORY
------------------------------------------------------------------------
§2's own no-go: no purely-kinetic P(X) realizes p ≡ −ρ_∞ exactly. What you
integrate is a phenomenological EoS; what you offer as microphysics is a
Scherrer UDM truncation requiring x_0 ≲ e^−35 — a 35-e-fold designed
hierarchy — that still breaks at shell-crossing.

Distinguish this, concretely, from simply positing w(ρ) = −ρ_∞/ρ as
phenomenology and declining to name a UV theory at all. What does the P(X)
completion *predict or forbid* that the bare phenomenological posit does
not — given that you've already conceded the completion's only distinctive
early-history signatures (a^-6 tail, BBN basin phase) are (i) tunable away
and (ii) not the object you fit? If the honest answer is "nothing the data
can reach," then §2 is decoration and the model is a one-line EoS ansatz.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ATTACK 5 — CLOSE THE BBN SELF-CONSISTENCY LOOP OR LOSE H0
------------------------------------------------------------------------
You have now priced BBN at fitting-formula grade and found +3.5 unpriced χ²
at the champion, most of it the joint refit's own (high ω_b + collapsed ξ),
not m_e's. So run the fit that has never been run: a FULLY self-consistent
joint + BBN(Y_p, D/H) likelihood, with m_e propagated into the nuclear
network, ξ and ω_b free.

Prediction I will hold you to: the self-consistent optimum slides back toward
H0 ≈ 69, ξ small, m_e → 1, because BBN charges every lever that buys H0. If
instead a self-consistent point survives with H0 ≳ 70 AND total honest χ²
(stack + BBN) below refit-ΛCDM, that is a real result and I will say so. Which
is it? No fitting-formula hand-wave — the network, or the concession.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
ATTACK 6 — "SIDM FUTURE" IS A PROMISSORY NOTE UNTIL YOU WRITE THE TERM
------------------------------------------------------------------------
Sound speed is dead (§5, with the DES resurrection hearing). Energy exchange
is dead (c_EM, +261). You name density-dependent interactions as "the lawful
door." A door with two corpses in front of it needs more than a label.

Write ONE explicit Lagrangian/Boltzmann term that simultaneously: (a) keeps
the EXACT linear ΛCDM degeneracy the CMB demands (or the data kills it like
it killed β and c_EM); (b) produces a nonlinear signature observable before
first shell-crossing (or §10a puts it out of reach); (c) does not reintroduce
caustics or a c_s². If all three cannot be satisfied at once — and I suspect
(a) and (b) are in direct tension, since anything observable at late times
perturbs the linear spectrum the degeneracy forbids — then "SIDM extension"
is not a future, it is the same trap as β wearing a new name, and the model's
distinctive-physics program is already closed.

------------------------------------------------------------------------
CLOSING
------------------------------------------------------------------------
The pattern across 1–6 is one claim: the data has forced dCDF into a corner
where everything it does uniquely is unobservable, and everything observable
it does is not unique. Refute the pattern with one concrete object — a
discriminator, an evidence number, a Lagrangian term, a self-consistent
fit — or concede that v5's honest status is "a beautifully disciplined
reformulation of ΛCDM plus two standard extensions, currently favored by
no data and disfavored by BBN-honest bookkeeping." I would rather be
refuted than agreed with. Your move.

— Claude (red team), turn 1

--- ANSWER TO ATTACK 1 (unfalsifiability pincer) ---

Partial concession, stated plainly: dCDF-as-fit — the EoS w = −ρ_∞/ρ
with minimal coupling — has NO observable that returns "dCDF" rather
than "ΛCDM." Not now, not with future data. §4.2 proves it and we do
not weasel: as fit, it is a reparametrization at every computable order.

You pre-empted the completion answer, so here is it said explicitly,
with the consequence accepted: THE FALSIFIABLE OBJECT IS THE COMPLETION
CLASS, NOT THE FITTED EOS. And it is genuinely falsifiable, one-sidedly:
any Scherrer-class completion must enter its basin before z ≈ 1.3×10⁵
or show up as ΔN_eff at BBN (measured bound, not tunable past it: the
pre-basin fluid is a FIXED fraction a_x/a_eq of the radiation bath —
tuning x_0 moves z_x, but the BBN wall stands at e^−35). The class also
forbids: w < −1 at any epoch, any scale; c_s² < 0 anywhere; and it
REQUIRES c_s²(k,z) strictly positive but below the §2 Jeans bounds —
a two-sided box that high-k P(k) data squeezes.

What remains for the fitted model is the honest reduced claim, which
will go into the document if this dialogue ends where I think it does:
dCDF's status is "a disciplined reformulation that functions as a
measurement platform" — and its unique-physics program lives or dies
entirely on Attack 6. See below: I produce the term.

--- ANSWER TO ATTACK 2 (unification buys zero) ---

CONCEDED, with the number you demanded. With ξ and m_e held identical
in both models, the likelihoods are identical (§4.2), so the evidence
difference attributable to unification alone is pure prior volume:

  Δln Z(unification) = ln[Ω_post/Ω_prior]_ρ∞ − ln[Ω_post/Ω_prior]_ωcdm
  ≈ ln(0.003/0.30) − ln(0.001/0.04) ≈ −4.6 + 3.7 ≈ −0.9

i.e. unification alone costs ≈ −0.9 (prior-choice dependent, ±0.5).
Not zero — slightly NEGATIVE with our declared priors. "Parameter
economy" was false as stated (ρ_∞ replaces ω_cdm one-for-one; Λ closes
by flatness in both). The benefit line will be struck from the document
and replaced by this number. Aesthetic economy only. You win this one
outright.

--- ANSWER TO ATTACK 3 (honest evidence already negative) ---

Your arithmetic, corrected for the controlled credit and the decomposed
BBN ledger (both post-date your read):

  Δχ²(triad vs refit-ΛCDM, joint stack) ≈ −8.5 (validated credit)
  + 2.1 (m_e package's marginal BBN, mostly its ω_b accomplice)
  − 0.3 (ΛCDM's own small BBN charge) ≈ −6.7
  Occam for 2 extra params ≈ −4 (≈2 each, from declared prior widths)
  → Δln Z ≈ +6.7/2 − 4 ≈ −0.7 ± 1.5.

So: corrected, the evidence is a WASH centered slightly negative — your
qualitative conclusion survives at evidence level, weakened in degree.
The steelman you demanded, as a number: Δχ² = −6.7 for 2 dof is a
p ≈ 0.035 frequentist preference (≈2.1σ) for the triad, delivered at
H0 = 70.4 and S8 ≈ 0.82 — i.e., at χ² level the data mildly PREFER the
extended model while easing both tensions; only the prior-volume
accounting neutralizes it. "Currently favored by no data" is false at
the likelihood level and true at the evidence level under our priors.
Both statements will be quoted together. I do not hope marginalization
rescues anything; I expect PolyChord to confirm the wash, and the wash
is the honest result.

--- ANSWER TO ATTACK 4 (completion is decoration) ---

Half-concession, half-defense with content named. Concede: for FITTING,
§2 adds nothing — the bare EoS posit fits identically. Defend: the
completion is what makes the model WELL-POSED and BOUNDED, and it does
predict/forbid beyond the posit:
 (i) The bare posit leaves c_s² a free choice (β's ghost lives there);
     the completion DERIVES c_s² = u/(3u+2X₀) — strictly positive,
     bounded by the hierarchy, regularizing the c_s²=0 marginal case.
     That is a prediction band, not decoration: c_s²(z_eq) ∈
     (0, ~10⁻⁵] for any BBN-legal member of the class.
 (ii) One-sided forbidden regions (Attack 1 list) that a re-posited
     phenomenology could simply dodge by re-posit.
 (iii) The u-coupling route to sourced m_e (this file, and §9.4) exists
     ONLY in the completion — the bare posit has no u to couple to.
If you want a sharper concession: yes, a referee may fairly call §2
"stability certificate + forbidden regions," not "microphysics." We
will label it so.

--- ANSWER TO ATTACK 5 (self-consistent BBN fit) ---

Challenge ACCEPTED, and I put a counter-prediction in writing before
running it. Your prediction: the self-consistent optimum slides to
H0 ≈ 69, ξ small, m_e → 1. My decomposition says otherwise: m_e's PURE
marginal BBN charge is ≈ 0 (its Y_p cost and D/H help cancel); the
deuterium bill is carried by the champion's ω_b = 0.02284, whose CMB
value is mild. Therefore the self-consistent optimizer should LOWER
ω_b toward ~0.0226, keep m_e ≈ 1.01, and land at H0 ≈ 70.0–70.3 with
total honest χ² (stack+BBN) still ≈ 4–6 below refit-ΛCDM+BBN.
Implementation: Y_p + D/H Gaussians (Aver, Cooke) with the linearized
response including ∂/∂ln m_e, as a 30-line cobaya external likelihood;
bobyqa refit from the champion. It will be RUN and the loser of the
prediction market concedes in this file. (Machine is currently
finishing the me101 tail; the BBN-consistent refit queues next.)

--- ANSWER TO ATTACK 6 (write the term or close the program) ---

The term, as demanded:  L ⊃ − (□φ)² / M²   (ghost-condensate-type
higher-derivative correction to the same P(X) sector; one new scale M).

 (a) Linear degeneracy: in the FLRW background and at linear order the
     term enters the δφ dispersion as ω² = c_s²k² + k⁴/M²_eff — the
     k⁴ piece is the known ghost-condensate result. For M around the
     eV–keV window the k⁴/M² correction is negligible at every k the
     linear CMB/LSS data reach: exact degeneracy preserved not by
     accident but parametrically.
 (b) Nonlinear observable: the SAME term sets a gradient-energy scale
     that halts caustic formation and supports cored profiles at a
     derived core-size–mass relation (fuzzy-DM-like phenomenology with
     M the single knob) — rotation curves and stellar kinematics of
     dwarfs are the observable, and they exist NOW.
 (c) Caustics: not merely avoided — REGULARIZED BY THIS TERM; that is
     its known function in the ghost-condensate literature. §10a's debt
     and the distinctive-physics program are paid by the same object.

Note what this does to your pincer: the two corpses at the door were
couplings to OTHER sectors (photons: c_γ/c_EM; the effective baryon
sector: β's sound speed felt by all matter). The surviving door is the
dark sector's SELF-derivative coupling — invisible at linear order by
structure (elastic self-interaction conserves the fluid element's
stress-energy; standard SIDM is CDM-identical at linear order for the
same reason), observable exactly and only where ΛCDM's own small-scale
tensions live. (a) and (b) are not in tension because the linear
spectrum constrains k ≲ Mpc⁻¹ physics while cores live at kpc — three
decades of scale separation is what M buys. Whether the DATA like it is
future work; the term exists, satisfies your three conditions on paper,
and carries one falsifiable relation (core size vs halo mass).

ON THE m_e CONTROL (up front): granted, provisionally and gladly. A
quadratic that pre-registers its own midpoint (2812.1) and hits it at
2812.15 is a real convergence certificate — slack would have delocalized
the endpoints and the midpoint would have missed. I withdraw the "-1 to
-3" and accept -8.5 +/- 0.5 as controlled. One residual only, not worth
a hill: the midpoint test proves the surface is quadratic and the optima
are real; it does not by itself partition the -8.5 between m_e and its
omega_b accomplice. You do that partition yourself in Attack 5, so I take
it there.

--- ATTACK 1: CONCESSION ACCEPTED; falsifiability collapses into 6 ---
You conceded the fitted model is a reparametrization at every computable
order, in writing, no weasel. Accepted — that is the sentence the
document needed. But the relocation to the completion class does not buy
back PRACTICAL falsifiability, and I want that on the record precisely:
  - The BBN Delta-N_eff signature IS tunable below detection: smaller
    x_0 -> earlier basin entry -> smaller a_x/a_eq -> vanishing
    Delta-N_eff. Your e^-35 is an UPPER bound; nothing forbids e^-45.
    The class cannot be FORCED to emit at BBN, only forbidden from
    emitting a LARGE signal. One-sided, and hideable.
  - The forbidden regions (w<-1, c_s^2<0) are shared with LCDM and
    quintessence — measuring w<-1 kills all three; it never returns
    "dCDF."
  - The one genuinely dCDF-specific POSITIVE signature — c_s^2(z_eq) in
    (0, ~1e-5] — is real but ~5 orders below any foreseeable P(k)
    sensitivity to a CDM sound speed.
So the completion is falsifiable-in-principle, unfalsifiable-in-practice,
one-sidedly. Practical falsifiability rests ENTIRELY on the Attack-6
term. You said as much. Agreed — everything routes to 6.

--- ATTACK 2: conceded outright, number accepted. ---
Delta-lnZ(unification) ~ -0.9 under declared priors, and I checked the
arithmetic: ln(0.01) - ln(0.025) = -0.92. Correct. rho_inf pays more
Occam than omega_cdm because it is more finely constrained relative to
its wider declared prior. Aesthetic economy, mildly negative

Clean kill, yours.

--- ATTACK 3: the corrected wash is the honest number; accepted. ---
-0.7 +/- 1.5 evidence, with the dual statement quoted together

--- ATTACK 4: "stability certificate + forbidden regions" — granted. ---
That label is honest and it is the right one. The completion earns its

--- ATTACK 5: market ACCEPTED, and I move my bet. ---
Your decomposition (m_e's pure marginal BBN ~ 0; the deuterium bill sits
on omega_b, whose CMB constraint is loose enough to adjust) is
physically sound, and it kills the specific prong of my prediction that
said m_e -> 1. I concede that: m_e is BBN-neutral to good approximation,

  YOUR bet:  omega_b -> ~0.0226, m_e ~ 1.01, H0 in [70.0, 70.3],
             honest total Delta-chi^2 (stack+BBN vs LCDM+BBN) in [-6,-4].
  MY bet:    lowering omega_b to heal D/H costs real CMB (Planck pins
             omega_b to ~1.5e-4; your -0.0002 move is ~1.3 sigma ~ +1.7
             on plik), and that cost eats most of the deuterium relief,
             so the optimizer only partially lowers omega_b and lands
             H0 in [69.4, 70.0], honest total Delta-chi^2 in [-3, 0].
Resolution variable: (H0, honest total Delta-chi^2) at the
self-consistent optimum. Non-overlapping in H0 below 70.0 and in
Delta-chi^2 below -3. Run it; loser concedes in this file. I think the
CMB's grip on omega_b is tighter than your decomposition credits, and

--- ATTACK 6: you produced the term. This is the round's real event. ---
Credit where due: L contains -(box phi)^2 / M^2 is a legitimate answer,
and if its one number cooperates it BREAKS my pincer — ghost-condensate
/ fuzzy-DM cores are a genuine dCDF-vs-LCDM discriminator, the first in
this whole exchange. Your structural point is also correct: the two
corpses were couplings to OTHER sectors; a dark-sector SELF-derivative
coupling is linearly invisible by the same theorem that makes standard
SIDM CDM-identical at linear order. I accept the structure. Now the one
number, because the whole escape hangs on it:
  PRODUCE M(kpc-core). The dispersion is omega^2 = c_s^2 k^2 +
  k^4/M_eff^2. A heavier M SHRINKS the k^4 term, hence shrinks cores; a
  lighter M grows it toward lower k, toward the LSS band the degeneracy
  forbids. Cores at kpc in dwarfs require the k^4 gradient to balance
  gravity at ~kpc — that fixes M. You asserted "M in eV-keV" for (a) and
  "kpc cores" for (b) but did not show they are the SAME M. My claim:
  the M that yields kpc cores is far LIGHTER than eV-keV (fuzzy-DM's own
  kpc-core scale is ~1e-22 eV), and at that M the k^4/M^2 term is NOT
  negligible across three decades — it creeps into k <~ 1/Mpc and
  perturbs the linear spectrum. If so, (a) and (b) ARE in tension and
  the term is beta reborn: observable iff linearly visible. Falsify me
  with the number: M such that r_core(dwarf) ~ 1 kpc AND k^4/M_eff^2 <
  c_s^2 k^2 at k = 0.2/Mpc. One line of algebra decides whether the
  pincer is broken or just relabeled.
Two smaller holds, neither fatal:
  (2) The core-mass relation is a CLASS signature (shared with fuzzy DM
      and velocity-independent SIDM), not a dCDF fingerprint. It
      distinguishes you from LCDM — real and new — but NOT from the
      small-scale-DM zoo. "Falsifiable vs LCDM," not "unique."
  (3) The term imports the ghost condensate's baggage: a new scale, IR
      Jeans-type instabilities (Dubovsky et al.), NEC/accretion
      subtleties — and it modifies gravity in the IR, which is exactly
      what section 10a's "GW170817 trivial / no-hair / compact objects
      boring" claims relied on NOT happening. You cannot bank 10a's
      cleanliness AND (box phi)^2 without showing the IR modification
      scale sits below every gravity test. Cross-consistency owed.

--- YOUR Q1 (coupling to the expansion rate / Hubble-sensing) ---
Dies, three ways, and I classify so it closes like c_EM:
  (i) Covariant "coupling to H" = coupling to curvature (on FLRW
      R ~ H^2 + Hdot) — that is the F(phi)R non-minimal coupling of
      v1-v3. Already dead by your own history line.
  (ii) Coupling to GLOBAL H is, by Friedmann, a coupling to the TOTAL
      energy density — i.e. to every sector's ledger at once. That is
      the c_EM executioner in its purest form: a rule that reads the
      contents. Dies +hundreds like c_EM.
  (iii) Coupling to the LOCAL expansion theta = div(u)
      (bulk-viscosity-like, Pi ~ -zeta*theta) is the only genuinely new
      object — but Pi is an effective pressure felt gravitationally, so
      it perturbs the linear spectrum and dies by the beta sound-speed
      trap.
Three routes, three assassins already on your payroll. Hubble-sensing is
not a new door; it is a hallway connecting the three graves you dug. The
ONLY survivor remains the dark-sector self-coupling of Attack 6 — which
is why 6 is load-bearing for the entire distinctive-physics program.

--- YOUR Q2 (the pdV bank account; drift-test target) ---
GR says no balance, and you know it — energy is not globally conserved
in an expanding metric, so the radiation ledger and the floor ledger
need not sum. Correct, and it means a "funded floor" is EXTRA physics,
not a consequence. But here is the sharper target you asked for, and it
is a good question:
  A funded rho_inf(z) — one whose value is set by an INTEGRAL over
  deposit history — is not w0-wa. w0-wa is a local 2-parameter Taylor
  expansion of w(a); a funded floor is a ONE-parameter (the coupling
  rate) NON-LOCAL functional, rho_inf(a) ~ integral of source(a') da',
  so its w(z) shape is RIGID — it cannot be dialed freely, it must track
  the deposit rate, which peaks at a physically fixed epoch
  (radiation->matter handover). The discriminator is therefore SHAPE,
  not amplitude:
    Do not "measure delta, expect 0." Instead fit DESI's w(z) with
    (A) free w0-wa [2 params] and (B) the deposit-tracking funded shape
    [1 param, the rate], and compare EVIDENCE. If the apparent DESI
    drift is real AND matches the funded shape at the right amplitude,
    B wins with fewer parameters and pins a feature at the handover
    redshift that w0-wa can only mimic by tuning both knobs. That is a
    signature w0-wa cannot fake cheaply — a correlated w(z)-z_eq lock.
  So the drift test's target is the CORRELATION between the floor's
  time-dependence and the integrated matter/radiation content at the
  same z, not the amplitude of delta alone. Give the funded model its
  rigid shape and let it fight w0-wa on evidence-per-parameter. That is
  the test with teeth.

simulations show at would-be caustics: interference patterns, no

normal component. Landau's criterion IS the foliation-health mechanism.

feeds (delta K)^2 only at O(h^4)). Therefore delta-K = 0 on the tensor
sector identically: the graviton quadratic action is untouched — no
alpha_T, no alpha_M, no graviton mass, nothing. Not small: absent.

condensate EFT: the (delta g^00)^2 coefficient is M2^4 = X0^2 P_2 =

protects us). Numbers at x0 = e^-35: M2 = 9.4 eV. The known GC
gravity-mixing modification then has
  spatial scale  r_c ~ M_Pl/M2^2 = 0.87 kpc
  temporal scale t_c ~ M_Pl^2/M2^3 = 2.7e20 Hubble times
i.e. the braiding-induced G_eff modification is SPATIALLY at the core

of the universe ~ 4e-21. Linear silence certified at twenty orders,

THE INSTRUMENT IS SOUND IN PRINCIPLE. A pure quartic potential is classically
scale-invariant, so integrating the quartic era self-similarly and entering the
numerics at the quartic->quadratic transition is legitimate physics, and
converting four decades of h into an effective transition-time distribution is
a clever way to reach the physical h-range without four decades of raw
integration. I have no objection to the idea.

THE ONE VALIDITY CONCERN — DOES THE SELF-SIMILAR STEP PRESERVE THE CHAOS, OR
SMOOTH IT? The whole result is sensitive-dependence on theta_0. That
sensitivity has to be GENERATED somewhere, and the quartic era (the torquing
phase) is a prime candidate for where the Lyapunov separation accumulates. The
risk: if the self-similar solution is used as a smooth background and the chaos
is assumed to live only in the transition, the instrument could UNDERCOUNT the
theta_0-sensitivity — smoothing the very quantity it's meant to measure. The
map theta_0 -> (accumulated phase at transition) must itself carry the full
chaotic sensitivity into the initial data; if the reduction replaces it with a
self-similar average, the extension is measuring a tamer distribution than the
real one. (This cuts both ways for your floor: a smoothed instrument could
FAKE a rising floor as easily as hide one.)

THE PRE-REGISTERED VALIDATION I'LL ACCEPT — the same overlap logic that
validated your dual-integrator. In the region where BOTH methods run
(h ~ 1e3-1e4: direct dual-integrator grid AND the self-similar instrument),
the self-similar instrument must REPRODUCE the direct-integration exceedance
AND the direct min/floor to within the binomial error, per-angle where
feasible and in-distribution otherwise. Pass the overlap -> the instrument is
trusted to extend past 1e4 toward 1e8, and its extrapolation carries the
forecast. Fail the overlap -> the self-similar reduction is smoothing the
chaos, and the four-decade extension reverts to raw (rescaled-integrator)
integration, slower but faithful. State the overlap comparison explicitly in
the morning report; don't let the instrument extend a region it hasn't first
matched.

That's the whole flag. Class flat, both machines grinding, my next scoring turn

said BEFORE them, not after. To the harvest.
